);</t><s>UPSERT INTO Art(id, title, artist, year) VALUES (1, 'Starry Night', 'Vincent van Gogh', 1889);</s>

<t>CREATE TABLE Art_Gallery (gallery_id INT PRIMARY KEY, gallery_name VARCHAR(255), location VARCHAR(255))

CREATE TABLE Artwork (artwork_id INT PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(255), artist VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10,2), gallery_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (gallery_id) REFERENCES Art_Gallery(gallery_id))</t><s>INSERT INTO Art_Gallery (gallery_id, gallery_name, location) VALUES (1, 'Gallery A', 'New York') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE gallery_name = 'Gallery A', location = 'New York';</s>

<t>CREATE TABLE artists (artist_id UUID PRIMARY KEY, artist_name STRING, art_style STRING)

CREATE TABLE paintings (painting_id UUID PRIMARY KEY, painting_title STRING, artist_id UUID REFERENCES artists(artist_id))

CREATE TABLE galleries (gallery_id UUID PRIMARY KEY, gallery_name STRING, location STRING) REFERENCES artists(artist_id))</t><s>UPSERT INTO artists (artist_id, artist_name, art_style) VALUES ('1', 'Vincent van Gogh', 'Post-Impressionism') ON CONFLICT (artist_id) DO UPDATE SET artist_name = excluded.artist_name, art_style = excluded.art_style;</s>

<t>CREATE TABLE artists (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    style VARCHAR(50)
);


CREATE TABLE artworks (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    artist_id INT NOT NULL,
    year_created INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artist_id) REFERENCES artists(id)
);


CREATE TABLE museums (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE exhibitions (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    museum_id INT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (museum_id) REFERENCES museums(id)
);


CREATE TABLE art_collections (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    artwork_id INT NOT NULL,
    collection_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artwork_id) REFERENCES artworks(id)
);

    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE artists (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    style VARCHAR(50)
);


CREATE TABLE art_collections (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    artwork_id INT NOT NULL,
    collection_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artwork_id) REFERENCES artworks(id)
);


CREATE TABLE exhibitions (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    museum_id INT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (museum_id) REFERENCES museums(id)
);
</t><s>upsert into artists (id, name, style) values (1, 'vincent van gogh', 'post-impressionism') on conflict (id) do update set name = 'vincent van gogh', style = 'post-impressionism';</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE artworks (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    artist_id INT NOT NULL,
    year_created INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artist_id) REFERENCES artists(id)
);

    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    artist_id INT NOT NULL,
    year_created INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artist_id) REFERENCES artists(id)
);


CREATE TABLE art_collections (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    artwork_id INT NOT NULL,
    collection_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artwork_id) REFERENCES artworks(id)
);


CREATE TABLE artists (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    style VARCHAR(50)
);


CREATE TABLE museums (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE exhibitions (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    museum_id INT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (museum_id) REFERENCES museums(id)
);

    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE exhibitions (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    museum_id INT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (museum_id) REFERENCES museums(id)
);
</t><s>upsert into artists (id, name, style) values (1, 'vincent van gogh', 'post-impressionism') on conflict (id) do update set name = 'vincent van gogh', style = 'post-impressionism';</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE art_collections (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    artwork_id INT NOT NULL,
    collection_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artwork_id) REFERENCES artworks(id)
);


CREATE TABLE artists (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    style VARCHAR(50)
);


CREATE TABLE artworks (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    artist_id INT NOT NULL,
    year_created INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artist_id) REFERENCES artists(id)
);


CREATE TABLE exhibitions (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    museum_id INT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (museum_id) REFERENCES museums(id)
);

    artwork_id INT NOT NULL,
    collection_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artwork_id) REFERENCES artworks(id)
);


CREATE TABLE exhibitions (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    museum_id INT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (museum_id) REFERENCES museums(id)
);


CREATE TABLE museums (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE artists (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    style VARCHAR(50)
);


CREATE TABLE artworks (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    artist_id INT NOT NULL,
    year_created INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artist_id) REFERENCES artists(id)
);
</t><s>upsert into artists (id, name, style) values (1, 'vincent van gogh', 'post-impressionism') on conflict (id) do update set name = 'vincent van gogh', style = 'post-impressionism';</s>

    name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    style VARCHAR(50)
);


CREATE TABLE museums (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE exhibitions (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    museum_id INT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (museum_id) REFERENCES museums(id)
);
</t><s>upsert into museums (id, name, location) values (1, 'louvre museum', 'paris, france') on conflict (id) do update set name = 'louvre museum', location = 'paris, france';</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE artworks (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    artist_id INT NOT NULL,
    year_created INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artist_id) REFERENCES artists(id)
);


CREATE TABLE art_collections (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    artwork_id INT NOT NULL,
    collection_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artwork_id) REFERENCES artworks(id)
);


CREATE TABLE artists (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,

    title VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    artist_id INT NOT NULL,
    year_created INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artist_id) REFERENCES artists(id)
);
</t><s>upsert into museums (id, name, location) values (1, 'louvre museum', 'paris, france') on conflict (id) do update set name = 'louvre museum', location = 'paris, france';</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE museums (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE exhibitions (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    museum_id INT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (museum_id) REFERENCES museums(id)
);


CREATE TABLE art_collections (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    artwork_id INT NOT NULL,
    collection_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artwork_id) REFERENCES artworks(id)
);

    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    artist_id INT NOT NULL,
    year_created INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artist_id) REFERENCES artists(id)
);


CREATE TABLE artists (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    style VARCHAR(50)
);


CREATE TABLE art_collections (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    artwork_id INT NOT NULL,
    collection_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    FOREIGN KEY (artwork_id) REFERENCES artworks(id)
);


CREATE TABLE exhibitions (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE,
    museum_id INT NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (museum_id) REFERENCES museums(id)
);


CREATE TABLE museums (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL
);
